Removed duplicates of file with Size: 1,4 GB

$awk '!seen[$0]++' boot_success_addr_output_complete.txt > boot_success_addr_output_complete_cleaned.txt


This Files shows 'all' reads and writes during boot process in the following address range:
addr > 0x2f000000 || addr < 0x84F0992

This are all reads/writes that occur during boot process w/o duplicates;
It seems to oscillate between the small addresses near the roms, the higher addresses that are not written by QEMU writes and the rootfs image file.
